## 3. Wayfinding Failures (Plus Signage/Paths/Regions)

- **Signage system**: numeric top-level folders signal sequencing, but intra-folder prefixes (`ARCH-`, `SCAFF-`, `DYN-`, `REF-`) are opaque without a legend.
- **Landmarks**: `CLAUDE.md`, `COCKPIT.md`, `CODEX.md`, `GEMINI.md` compete as landmarks; none is marked as primary.
- **Paths**: expected path “start -> overview -> operate” breaks because entry points do not consistently link to `00-ORCHESTRATION/`, `02-ENGINE/`, or `03-QUEUE/`.
- **Regions**: `05-MEMORY/` and `-OUTGOING/` represent overlapping “done” regions, weakening regional boundaries.
- **Where wayfinding fails**: acronym-heavy names, parallel archives, and limited cross-links create dead ends for new agents.
- **Progressive disclosure**: Layer 0 (root entry files) exists, but Layer 1 overview is fragmented; Layer 2 details are deep and acronymic; Layer 3 deep knowledge exists but lacks signposted paths.
- Low-clarity names (score <=3) likely cold trails for new agents: `.DS_Store`, `.gitignore`, `.gitattributes`, `-INBOX/.DS_Store`, `00-ORCHESTRATION/.DS_Store`, `02-ENGINE/.DS_Store`, `.tmp.driveupload/15627`, `06-EXEMPLA/.DS_Store`, `.claude/.DS_Store`, `04-SOURCES/.DS_Store` ...

## 5. Affordance Gaps

- The presence of `Makefile` suggests operational automation, but there is no discoverable “how to run” pointer from entry points.
- `-OUTGOING/` suggests a single export channel, yet there are multiple outgoing paths (root and within project).
- `00-ORCHESTRATION/blackboard/` implies a shared system state, but it is not linked from entry points.
- `03-QUEUE/` suggests actionable work, but queue disposition and actual queue contents are separated without clear routing.
- `06-EXEMPLA/` provides templates but is not referenced from entry points, lowering its affordance visibility.

## 7. Mental Model Diagram

```
Designer Model (implied)
  Entry -> Orchestration (00) -> Canon (01) -> Operational (02) -> Queue (03) -> Sources (04) -> Archive (05) -> Exempla (06)

System Model (actual)
  Multiple entry points (CLAUDE/COCKPIT/CODEX/GEMINI)
  Parallel storage: 05-MEMORY + -OUTGOING + root -OUTGOING
  Mixed prefixes across orchestration, state, directives, execution logs
  Deep nested sub-systems: prompts, models, registries, scripts, sources/raw/processed

User Model (newcomer inference)
  Start at CLAUDE/COCKPIT -> get lost in acronym-heavy folders
  Unsure whether to read CANON or OPERATIONAL first
  Unsure where “final” work lives (Archive vs Outgoing)

Divergence Points
  - Entry point primacy
  - Archive vs Outgoing semantic overlap
  - Acronym prefix opacity
```


## 8. Refactoring for Navigability (Recommendations)

- Declare a single canonical entry (`START_HERE.md`) that links to role-based trails (reader, operator, contributor).
- Introduce a “navigation spine” README at repo root with a 1-screen overview and a map of top-level directories.
- Consolidate “outgoing” paths into one canonical export directory; add a lightweight index file.
- Adopt explicit naming expansions for acronym prefixes (e.g., `ARCH-` -> `ARCHITECTURE-`).
- Add cross-links: `06-EXEMPLA/README.md` should be linked from entry points and operational protocols.
- Create mini-README.md per major directory to reduce intrinsic load by summarizing purpose and contents.
